         function showlegalparam() {
                      if (localStorage.getItem("uid")) {
                        var showlegal = localStorage.getItem("showlegal") || "";
                        $(".showlegalparam").each(function() {
                          var s, $this = $(this);
                          if (s = $this.attr("href")) {
                            $this.attr("href",
                              s.split("&showlegal=")[0]
                               + "&showlegal=" + showlegal);
                          }
                          if (s = $this.attr("data-link")) {
                            $this.attr("data-link",
                              s.split("&showlegal=")[0]
                               + "&showlegal=" + showlegal);
                          }
                         });
                      }
                    };
                    $(showlegalparam);

   <script>
    $(function() {
   if (localStorage.getItem('showlegal') == '1') {
     $('.js_cookie').slideDown(500);
     $('.js_agree').on('click', function(){
       $('.js_cookie').slideUp(500);
       localStorage.removeItem('showlegal');
       dataLayer.push({'showlegal': null});
       if (showlegalparam)
         showlegalparam();
     });
     $('.js_close-cookie').on('click', function() {
       $('.js_cookie').slideUp(500);
       localStorage.setItem('showlegal', '0');
       if (showlegalparam)
         showlegalparam();
     });
     $('.js_read-more-cookies').on('click', function() {
       $('.js_cookie p').addClass('open');
       $('.only-mobile').remove();
     });
   }
 });
